// [s dyz | fxyz]
if ( !((g_upper_bound_factors[abc.x] * g_auxiliary_upper_bound_factors[primitive_index_c] * fabs(d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+5)]) < schwarz_screening_threshold) && (!is_prim_id_neq || g_upper_bound_factors[abc.x] * g_auxiliary_upper_bound_factors[primitive_index_c] * fabs(d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index)]) < schwarz_screening_threshold))) {
	val = coefAndNorm * 0.03125*p*(c->coordinate.x - Rp[0])*(-16.0*p*(a->coordinate.y - b->coordinate.y)*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(2.0*Boys[3]*p*(a->coordinate.z - b->coordinate.z)*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[3]*sum_exp - 2.0*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2]))) + 16.0*p*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(2.0*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(-c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(-Boys[4]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[5]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])) + (a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp*(-Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp + Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2]))) + sum_exp*(-Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp + Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1]))) + 16.0*p*(a->coordinate.z - b->coordinate.z)*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp*(Boys[3]*sum_exp + 2.0*p*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*(Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.y - Rp[1])*sum_exp - Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.y - Rp[1]))) - 8.0*sum_exp*(Boys[3]*sum_exp + 2.0*p*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*(Boys[3]*(a->coordinate.z - Rp[2])*sum_exp - Boys[4]*c->exponent*(c->coordinate.z - Rp[2]))))/(sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp*sum_exp) ;
	val *= d_cgto_normalization_factors[a->basis_index] * d_cgto_normalization_factors[b->basis_index] * d_auxiliary_cgto_normalization_factors[c->basis_index];
	atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(a->basis_index) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+9], val * d_C_diff_vector[(b->basis_index+5)]);
	if(is_prim_id_neq) atomicAdd(&d_W_diff[(b->basis_index+5) * num_auxiliary_basis + c->basis_index+9], val * d_C_diff_vector[(a->basis_index)]);
}
